The Public Works Bureau and the Shanghai Gas Company Concluded a Franchise Contract 129

Term of Forty Years

Since 1916, the Shanghai Gas Company has paid the Public Works Bureau 1,000 taels of silver every year. In recent years, gas street lights have almost disappeared, and the use of gas is mainly for household use. The Public Works Bureau has decided that the time has come to regulate the company's business with a franchise contract. Therefore, in March of this year, it concluded a contract with the company, which has been implemented since January 1 of this year. The main terms are that after the company's gross income from gas sales in the Concession and roads outside the Concession, after deducting the annuity payable to the Chinese authorities, 5% should be reported to the Public Works Bureau and paid every six months. The contract is for a term of forty years. Every ten years, the Public Works Bureau may notify the company one year in advance to purchase the company's business and real estate in the Concession. The purchase price will be properly settled by both parties at that time, or publicly assessed by arbitrators. The detailed terms of the contract will be published in today's Public Works Bureau Municipal Gazette.

Pudong Yangjiadu China Merchants Bureau - Barge Owners Scuffle Over Cargo Transportation 130

Zhou Lin's Violent Actions Lead to Major Disaster; Yang Zhanglin's Bones Broken, Life in Critical Condition

Around 9:00 AM on the morning of the day before yesterday, a major case of armed fighting and severe injury occurred in front of the warehouse of the China Merchants Bureau wharf in Yangjiadu, Pudong. The details are as follows:

Cause of the Dispute: Zhou Linsheng, the head of a barge fleet, owns over ten barges and contracts for the transportation of soybean and soybean cake for the Changde Oil Factory. This spring, Zhou Qiang wanted the Changde Oil Factory to increase the barge transportation wages, but they were not approved. Therefore, the factory terminated the contract and selected another barge operator, Chen, to take over the contract. Zhou harbored resentment towards Chen for seizing his business and publicly threatened to kill Chen.

Details of the Assault: Around 9:00 AM on the morning of the day before yesterday, Chen, under the orders of the factory, instructed his crew member Yang Zhanglin (55 years old, from Pudong) to go to the China Merchants Bureau warehouse in Yangjiadu, Pudong, to load soybeans. Zhou found out about this and ordered his chief steward, nicknamed "Little Old Third" Jin Sheng, to gather over ten Shandong workers, each armed with iron bars and other weapons. They went to the wharf and held Yang down. They first knocked him to the ground, and then violently struck Yang's chest and back with iron bars, breaking several ribs and back bones. Yang immediately fell to the ground, unconscious. The warehouse clerk urgently blew the police whistle, and the police arrived and arrested "Little Old Third" Jin Sheng. Zhou Linsheng and others managed to escape.

Life in Critical Condition: In addition to detaining and sending the suspect to the Yangjiadu Public Security Bureau, the police sent the injured person to Pudong Hospital. The doctor determined that the injuries were severe and life-threatening and transferred him to the Qu-surname trauma hospital in Puxi for treatment. However, his leg bones were already broken, and he was spitting up blood non-stop. Furthermore, Yang is already in his sixties, and he has fainted several times yesterday, and his life is feared to be in danger.

Transfer to Court: The Chief of the Yangjiadu Public Security Bureau interrogated the suspect "Little Old Third" Jin Sheng. As the matter concerned injury, he immediately prepared a document to transfer the suspect to the District Court. After a preliminary hearing by the duty prosecutor, he ordered the suspect to be detained, pending an examination of Yang's injuries before further legal action. Meanwhile, warrants were issued to apprehend the principal offender and accomplices for thorough investigation.

Over Sixty Organizations Jointly Petition the Public Works Department, Opposing Telephone Price Increase 131

Requesting the Board of Directors to Reconsider, Minimum Requirement is to Postpone Implementation

The Shanghai First and Second Special District Citizens' Federation, along with its district branches, the Chinese National Products Manufacturers Federation, and various hometown associations, totaling over sixty organizations, are concerned that the issue of telephone price increases has not been resolved, causing anxiety among users and hindering commercial development. They have jointly signed a letter to the Board of Directors of the Public Works Department to continue their efforts to oppose the price increase. The letter states: To the Esteemed Board of Directors, regarding the Shanghai Telephone Company of the Public Concession,

Repeated Price Increases: The Chinese and foreign people within the concession have repeatedly expressed their opposition. Our federation and other organizations, as representatives of citizens and various business sectors, have each expressed our firm opposition based on the opinions of our members and the public. However, the matter has not reached a conclusion, causing anxiety among users and preventing them from using telephones as they wish. The effectiveness of telephones has been diminishing invisibly, hindering communication to an extreme. Therefore, we dare to jointly send this letter to your esteemed board, presenting the simple reasons as follows: (1) The current situation in Shanghai has reached a state of extreme decline. Few businesses can barely maintain their operations. Further increasing the burden is unbearable. The Shanghai Telephone Company already has profits to gain and is in a better position than ordinary businesses. It should share the hardships with its users and should not necessarily achieve its budgeted goals by raising prices again. (2) Telephones are a public utility, with the purpose of facilitating the public. Profits should be limited. Regardless of whether it is in China or foreign countries, there is no public utility that must guarantee a certain level of profit. Why does the Shanghai Telephone Company make such a harsh demand, and why does your bureau allow it? Furthermore, a contract has been signed allowing them to repeatedly increase prices. Although we are not aware of the exact wording of the contract, your Director-General stated that "failure to allow the price increase would damage credibility." We believe that the fulfillment of this contract should be subject to the opinions of the majority of users and be changed according to the social environment. It should be treated as an exception to ordinary contracts. (3) Furthermore, how does the Shanghai Telephone Company's

Profit and Loss Actually Look? Before ordinary users have the opportunity to truly understand its actual contents, it is difficult to believe that the company needs to raise prices. (4) The Shanghai Telephone Company has declared that it needs to raise prices due to excessive capital investment and high expenses. However, according to commercial practice, the higher the price, the more difficult it is to sell. It is better to have small profits and quick turnover to promote sales. The company only knows how to spend money on advertising and promotion but cannot see that it can increase profits by reducing prices. This is a clumsy plan. As for expenses, they may not be impossible to reduce. (5) The price increase method, calculated by the number of calls, is even more unlimited. According to our investigation of the actual usage of various users, the cost will exceed the original price by two or three times. Although your bureau has not yet approved it, allowing it to increase by 125 is in fact also unbearable for users. We request your bureau to reconsider. At a minimum, it must be changed to postpone implementation. (6) The so-called

Postponing Implementation: Of course, it means that your bureau should negotiate with the Shanghai Telephone Company to delay the price increase until a certain number of months or years later. In any case, it cannot be approved for the company to retroactively charge the new price, even if your bureau allows the company to approve it on a certain date, it must still retroactively charge the new price from April 1 of this year. In short, the directors of your bureau are indeed talented and wise men, who represent the taxpayers of the concession and govern the municipality. However, the actual situation of the people may not be fully known. We ask the directors to adopt the opinions of the people, weigh the importance of the matter, and not lightly agree to the demands of one company while disregarding the hardships of the majority of users. Otherwise, regardless of whether they are telephone users, all taxpayers in the Public Concession, for the sake of past suffering and future welfare, may have unfortunate events occur that we do not want to mention and that the directors do not want to hear. The harm will not only be limited to the Shanghai Telephone Company alone. We hope you will understand this and make a decisive decision to quickly determine a solution to continue communication and promote public welfare. To the Board of Directors of the Shanghai Public Concession Public Works Department,

Aurora University - Rumors of Red Light Ghost Fire - Lights Reflecting Off Red Glass Windows; Rumor-Mongers Exploiting the Situation 132

Aurora University, located at the intersection of Ningbo Road and Route Tenant de May, in the French Concession, is established by the French Municipal Council to specifically educate Chinese children. About a week ago, the patrolling Annamese police discovered a blazing red light on the roof of the school at night and mistook it for a fire. It seemed to be coming from the back. The police immediately went to De Xing Li behind the school to check and found no fire. For the sake of security, the police reported to the police station, which notified the fire brigade to rush to the scene to check, but there was still nothing unusual. However, the red light was still sometimes bright and sometimes dim, and some busybodies passing by immediately started rumors that red light ghost fire had been discovered on the upper floor of Aurora University, sometimes bright and sometimes dim. As a result, hundreds of passersby have been stopping to watch every night in recent days. The rumors started and grew from sunset to late at night, with the number of viewers increasing. According to the school's faculty and staff, who are all Catholic priests, there are lights on the upper floor. Recently, the wind has been blowing on the red glass windows, and the firelight reflected on the glass, leading to this rumor. The night before last, the French police sent Chinese, Western, and Annamese police to block the section of Ningbo Road from Bali Bridge Road to Route Tenant de May, preventing pedestrians from passing. At the same time, they notified the school to close the windows, and the red light disappeared, and the rumors also subsided.

Xu Changrong Suddenly Surrenders to Avoid Harming His Guarantor 134

The Third Trial Concludes with a Fine of Two Thousand Dollars and a Prison Sentence of One Year and Four Months

Xu Changrong, a local resident nicknamed "Xu Xiao Kai," who lives at 423 Rue Lanville, Tangjiawan, French Concession, and runs a physical store, is 34 years old this year. He was arrested by the French police in the autumn of the 22nd year of the Republic of China for jointly organizing a lottery gambling house and serving as the accountant. He was prosecuted by the Second Special Court and sentenced to one year and six months in prison and fined two thousand dollars. Xu disagreed with the original verdict and appealed. He was detained in the Second Special Court Detention Center. Due to illness, he requested the Third High Branch Court to stop the detention. He was ordered to pay a cash guarantee of four thousand dollars and provide a surety who would be available at any time. After being released on bail, the case was to be enforced, but Xu avoided appearing in court. It was decided to confiscate the guarantee money and issue an arrest warrant, which has been reported in previous newspapers. Separately, the Third High Branch Court issued another arrest warrant and sent police to arrest Xu's guarantor, Yao Gui, and detain him, setting a deadline for Xu to be handed over to the court. At this point, Xu realized that harming others and himself could not be resolved by hiding. Suddenly, yesterday, Xu voluntarily reported to the Third High Branch Court to request execution. The execution court of the High Court, presided over by Judge Pan Peien, opened the court and ordered Xu Changrong to be brought to court. After briefly questioning his age and origin, the court announced the third trial verdict, which was still one year and six months in prison. After deducting the number of days previously detained in the detention center, with two days offsetting one day of imprisonment, he should serve one year, four months, and seventeen days, and must pay the fine of two thousand dollars within a specified period. Xu obeyed the order, and the bailiffs immediately took Xu down and sent him to prison for execution.

Shanghai Yearbook Published 136

At the end of last year, the Shanghai Municipal Archives, entrusted by the Municipal Government, edited the "Shanghai Yearbook of the Republic of China, 24th Year" The Museum immediately established the Shanghai Yearbook Committee in January of this year, devoting all its efforts to it. According to the original plan, the book would be published at the end of April, and it has now been realized. The entire book contains 1.8 million words, divided into special reports, major event summaries, regional evolution, population, weather, party affairs, administration, judiciary, foreign affairs, military affairs, finance, public boundaries, French Concession, finance, education, transportation, industry, labor, commerce, agriculture, forestry, fisheries and animal husbandry, academics, religion, social undertakings, current events diary, and a list of celebrities (more than 3,700 people). The entire Shanghai has been dissected vertically and horizontally by the yearbook. The entire book has 1,300 pages and a special price of only two yuan.

Liu's Preface: The book features a handwritten inscription by former Mayor Wu and a preface by Liu Yazi, the director of the museum, which states, "In the third year of my tenure as the director of the Shanghai Municipal Archives, the compilation of the Shanghai Yearbook began. Now that the compilation is complete, my colleagues have asked me for a word. I believe that the books of local chronicles in China are abundant, but few authors are capable of writing them well. The best ones are only comparable to historical materials and are mostly half-baked and unrefined. The worst ones are simply cut and paste from outdated newspapers. The Shanghai Municipal Archives is the first organization to study local historical materials using scientific methods and should be listed as a permanent institution. The members of the editorial department work diligently day and night, racking their brains and dedicating themselves to studying Shanghai as a lifelong career. Looking back four thousand years and across ninety thousand miles, there is hardly any comparison. The draft of the general history is expected to be completed in four or five years. The yearbook started this year, and I privately hope that it will be compiled every year without end, so that people all over the world will know why Shanghai is Shanghai and that it will be beneficial to the progress of world culture. If there are enlightened people in the world who do not dismiss these words as irrelevant,

The Compilation Process: From January 1, 1935 (Republic of China 24th Year), most of the members of the Shanghai Yearbook Committee devoted all their efforts to the compilation, extending their working hours from eight hours to ten hours per day. The compilation rules are as follows: 1. This yearbook takes the unified ten tables as the center and is supplemented by text. This is because statistical tables represent the most recent, true, and difficult-to-misrepresent information. Those who are familiar with statistical tables can usually discern whether the numbers or text are correct and genuine. The statistical tables in this yearbook that require comparison will also list the comparison statistics. All statistical tables strive to be for the Republic of China 23rd year (1934). If the enterprise itself does not yet have statistics for the Republic of China 23rd year (1934), then the most recent statistical tables will be used. 2. Each enterprise briefly describes its evolution in order to show the traces of its development. (The information on this evolution is based on the museum's usual research and may be more accurate.) 3. The sources of all materials must be clearly stated to show the basis of the material and to express our gratitude for using the material. 4. The Gregorian calendar dates are mostly attached below the Chinese calendar dates to facilitate calculation. 5. Foreign names and place names are annotated with their original names, except when it is impossible to ascertain their original names, for verification purposes. 6. The writing style uses simple classical Chinese to save space, and new-style punctuation is used for easy reading. What makes us most happy is that the materials requested from all parties have been delivered continuously, either as tables or as files, which are detailed and accurate. The members of the committee then organized them one by one, and those without statistics were compiled by the committee, and those with statistics were repeatedly proofread. The museum originally published a periodical that was completely given away to all sectors of society. However, the costs of typesetting and printing the Shanghai Yearbook are extremely high, and it is sold at a special price, so it will not be given away except to related institutions.

The Company Decides to Produce Nitric Acid First, with Formal Deliveries to Start in Two Months

Their fellow villager Shen Yunsheng, who usually did not engage in honest work, only knew how to profit and did not hesitate to commit heinous acts. On March 2nd of this year, Shen falsely told his aunt Yang in his hometown that his cousin A'e, who was 16 years old, should not sit idle at home. He intended to take her to Shanghai to find a factory job. Once she got a job, she would be able to make a profit. Yang was deceived and ordered her daughter A'e to go to Shanghai with Shen's family. During the journey, Shen was lustful and lingered in the area, temporarily staying in a hostel, and the woman's chastity was violated. Shen's funds were not sufficient. After staying in Shuangling for two days, his travel expenses were running out. After satisfying his lust, he continued with his original plan, brought the woman to Shanghai, and discussed the matter with the pimps Xu Axiang and Amao. They agreed to send A'e to the brothel, stipulating that she would work as a prostitute for four months, and Xu would give Shen a deposit of 20 yuan. From then on, the young woman from a good family became a common prostitute. The pimps only wanted to ensure that they had an income every night, so they supervised A'e to welcome new customers and send off old ones, extremely strictly. If there was an empty night, she would be whipped severely. A weak woman who was not fully developed was subjected to this destruction, not only contracting syphilis but also becoming increasingly frail. The woman was trapped in hell, unable to escape. Recently, she met a customer who happened to be from her hometown. She confided in him about the circumstances of her fall, begging for help. The customer was a chivalrous and righteous person and was related to Su Xiao as a fellow villager. He generously agreed to help and immediately sent a letter to A'e's mother, Yang, urging her to come to Shanghai as soon as possible. The other day, Yang arrived in Shanghai, and the customer arranged for the woman to be taken away from the prostitutes and opened a room at the Zhongshan Hotel on Tianjin Road so that the mother and daughter could meet and confide in each other. They determined that the culprit was Shen Yunsheng. They reported the information to the Xinzha Police Station, which sent detective Wu Changkai to investigate the thousand criminals. When they went to arrest Shen, they learned that he had already fled and was missing. Xu Axiang, Xu Amao, who had privately set up a brothel and forced good women into prostitution, and Yang Lianhua, who had been raised as a private prostitute, were arrested and detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the District Court of the First Special District. Judge Liu Yugui interrogated them. Police lawyer Qian Jiuchen explained the case. The pimps still tried to deny it, but A'e testified about the various circumstances of being forced into prostitution and frequently being abused. Judge Liu then ordered A'e to be sent to a forensic doctor to determine the condition of her venereal disease. Her mother, Yang, was allowed to take her back, and the defendants were still detained to await a scheduled sentencing.

Director Cai's Notice - Beware of Imposters Investigating Drugs 141

Shanghai Municipal Police Department Director Cai issued a notice yesterday, stating: "It has been reported that recently, there have been incidents of people impersonating personnel from this bureau, entering shops under the guise of searching for drugs, and taking the opportunity to rob. This is extremely hateful. Investigations of criminal suspects should be conducted with an order from a superior officer and in conjunction with the local police officer. Therefore, whether they are personnel from this bureau can be determined by whether they have an order from a superior officer and are accompanied by a uniformed police officer. From now on, if any household in this city encounters someone claiming to be personnel from this bureau dispatched to search without a superior officer or a uniformed police officer accompanying them, they should immediately refuse and may report to the local police officer for investigation in order to prevent criminals and secure the safety of the residents. This notice is hereby issued for general knowledge."

Bicycles Allowed to Travel in Five Provinces and Cities 143

Exempt from Local Donations

The Traffic Committee of the five provinces and cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Beijing, and Shanghai believes that bicycles are economical and convenient and are suitable for short-distance travel. They are particularly effective in connecting transportation in the suburbs of cities. Therefore, the committee feels that it is necessary to promote bicycle transportation. Furthermore, because China's connecting highways are developing and the scope of interconnection is expanding, the committee decided at its ninth regular meeting that "vehicles registered and taxed by vehicle owners in their respective provinces and cities shall be allowed to travel in other provinces and cities without being charged additional transit fees or interconnection donations." It also requested the authorities of the five provinces and cities to announce and implement this decision and to separately propose measures to promote bicycles and their manufacturing to facilitate progress. From now on, bicycles within the scope of the five provinces and cities only need to pay the tax and fees in accordance with the regulations in their place of registration once and can travel without obstruction. In addition, the committee stated that the Shanghai China National Road Construction Association will hold a bicycle driving competition on the 12th of this month, which is in line with the committee's aim to promote bicycle transportation. It has specially made nine silver shields with safety shield designs and nine copies of the meeting minutes, which will be awarded to the top three in each group. The Road Association has already displayed them at the China Underwear Company on South Nanjing Road.

Small World: Temporary Reopening After Reorganization 145

Reopening Scheduled Today, Supported by Various Entertainment Groups

Small World, located on Fuyou Road in the city, has been around for many years. However, due to the recent economic downturn, business has been sluggish, and it has been in a state of decline. Recently, the city's Bureau of Education's Drama Review Committee deemed the Siming Opera performances at the venue to be immoral and ordered the entertainment venue to suspend performances for three days. After receiving the order, the venue convened a shareholders' meeting. Due to the poor market conditions and years of losses, the shareholders were not interested in continuing operations and entrusted lawyer Lu Ruizheng to announce the liquidation on the 24th of last month. This affected the livelihoods of more than 1,000 performers and staff members of the entertainment venue, causing panic. They went to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to petition for assistance, which yielded very satisfactory results. They then went to the board of directors and lawyer Lu to request assistance in maintaining their livelihoods. Businesses in the vicinity of the entertainment venue have also found it difficult to stay open after Small World closed. It is now reported that the board of directors of the entertainment venue, in order to maintain the livelihoods of the performers and staff, has decided to temporarily reopen during the liquidation period. Representatives from various entertainment groups will work with lawyer Lu and manager Yu Gengsheng to handle all matters. The interior has been completely renovated, and normal operations will resume as of today (the 3rd).

After receiving the confession, Bureau official Liu immediately ordered the local保甲 to report to the local court for an examination. He also sent a message to transfer the five Russians to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Zhu Xuefan: Labor Day Speech 147

Expanding Literacy Education, Indicating the Path of Struggle for Workers

The Shanghai General Labor Union commemorated May Day by holding a memorial meeting. Chairman Zhu Xuefan also delivered a speech at the Central and Western Radio Station at 4:00 PM, outlining the path of struggle for workers and promoting labor literacy education. His words were very encouraging. The transcript of his speech is as follows: Fellow compatriots, comrades, all workers in Shanghai, all workers in the country, today is May 1st, International Labor Day, commemorating the successful "Sanba" (three eights) movement launched by American workers in 1886. Fifty years ago, American workers suffered greatly under the oppression of capitalists. Unable to bear the oppression and destruction of capitalists, they launched the Labor Day movement in 1886, demanding the "Sanba" system. The American workers were indeed victorious. From May 1st of that year, the "Sanba" system of eight hours of work, eight hours of education, and eight hours of rest was implemented. We must know that in the year before the demand for the "Sanba" system, in 1885, several workers who led the movement in Chicago were sentenced to death by the government. At the time of their execution, they shouted loudly and fearlessly, "The time will come when our silence in the grave will be more moving than our speeches." We believe that they sacrificed their blood and heads for the welfare of workers and for the happiness of the masses. When they were executed, they were still so brave and righteous. This spirit of regarding death as returning home is really worthy of admiration and emulation. Today, the "Sanba" system can be implemented in most countries in the world, which is the result of their efforts. Laborers all over the world commemorate the sacrificed martyrs and commemorate the success of the "Sanba" system, which is the commemoration of this May Day. We in China only had this memorial day and the memorial ceremony in the seventh year of the Republic of China. Our President Sun was one of the most enthusiastic advocates of May Day. President Sun worked hard to find a way out for the workers, to seek welfare for the workers, to relieve the suffering and oppression of the workers, and to save the laborers of all of China. Therefore, he worked hard to promote May Day, worked hard to shout for the "Sanba" system, and launched the workers' movement. Therefore, the Chinese workers' movement relied on this seed to develop and grow to this day. We all know that the Chinese workers' movement is most historical, glorious, and great in Shanghai. However, it has now turned into a period of decline. We know that the workers' movement in Shanghai only started after the May Fourth Movement in the eighth year of the Republic of China. That period can be regarded as the first stage, which can be called the germination period. The workers' organization and training, the spirit and strength of struggle, are gradually developing. After the May 30th Massacre in the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, it entered the first stage, which we can call the enlightenment period. In order to resist the oppression of imperialism and the exploitation of capitalists, workers spontaneously organized and used a firm spirit, selfless long struggles, and sacrifices to create the foundation of the workers' movement. After the National Revolutionary Army arrived in Shanghai in the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, the workers' movement entered the third stage, which can be regarded as the golden period. The workers' organization and training, the workers' strength and spirit, were fully expressed, which released a brilliant flower in the history of the labor movement in Shanghai and became a great enemy of imperialist capitalists. If we can carry on this spirit, the future development will be increasingly expanded. However, since the "September 18th Incident" in the twentieth year of the Republic of China and the "January 28th Incident" in the twenty-first year, the workers' movement has declined, the welfare of the workers has rarely developed, and the power of the workers has declined day by day. The labor movement in Shanghai is also like the setting sun on the Western Hills, declining and depressed. This is roughly the process of the labor movement in Shanghai, which can also be said to be the history of the development of the labor movement in the whole of China. What is the workers' movement in the whole of China now? What is the workers' movement in Shanghai now? Declining, the same decline. We see that the workers in Shanghai are now implementing the "Sanba" system, are they living a stable life? We know that not only has the "Sanba" system not been implemented, but no one hires them even if they are willing to work twelve hours a day, and no one pays attention to them even if they are willing to do heavy work for the lowest wages. As for a stable life, that is even more out of the question. What is the reason for this? We know that our country is suffering from the oppression and aggression of imperialist economy, the rural economy is bankrupt, industry and commerce are declining, there is a huge amount of unfavorable balance of trade, and silver is flowing out, resulting in the current economic crisis. Therefore, factories are closing down and workers are unemployed. The entire nation and the entire country are trapped in a critical period. It is really difficult to solve the labor problem alone. Therefore, the workers' movement has declined, and the workers have silently and quietly laid down. We see that the Second Factory and the Fifth Factory of the Shenxin Textile Company, which is known as our national industry, have not yet started work, and the Seventh Factory has not yet been resolved after being unreasonably auctioned off by HSBC. The oppression of the imperialist economy has damaged our national industry. Even large factories like Shenxin cannot withstand it. Other small capital factories and shops are naturally unable to save it. We see that many factories and shops are either closing down automatically or being sealed by the court. This phenomenon really makes us feel sad. The entire market situation in China is now like this. How can the workers in Shanghai and the workers in the whole country implement the "Sanba" system? In reality, it cannot be discussed in China at present. China's unfavorable balance of trade from the eighth year of Tongzhi to the twenty-third year of the Republic of China totaled 1,090,591,000 流 out. We think that in the past 66 years, there has been such a large number, which is really appalling. China has such a vast land, such abundant products, such a large population, and such a profound culture, but it just keeps sending money to foreign countries day by day and cannot think of a way to collect it back. It has been reduced to this disabled scene. Can we not be pessimistic? But pessimism is useless. We must recognize the most important reason for the current situation. We must make fundamental remedies from this reason. What is the biggest reason for the Chinese crisis? That is, illiteracy and lack of education. (To be continued)

Another Opinion: I visited the London Art Exhibition preview once last week. On April 30th, because I got a group discount, I asked to see it again. That is, this cart for selling goods can be seen everywhere in small cities, which is enough to prove that our social situation and material civilization have not made much progress for thousands of years. How can we catch up with the trend of the world? Alas, everyone, hurry up and work hard." I think this scholar can observe the social evolution problem from the art with his calm mind and keen eyes. Searching for the taste outside the taste, the old man can't be unique in front of me. The Central Bank's 231st inspection report on issuance preparation stated that the association is responsible for inspecting the reserve for exchange coupons issued by the bank in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations. The 231st inspection was held in the bank's issuance bureau on April 30, 1935. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) The total amount of exchange coupons issued is 92,031,583 yuan in silver, including 85,077,688 yuan in silver coupons and 6,953,895 yuan in subsidiary currency coupons. The total amount of exchange coupon reserves is 92,031,583 yuan, including 73,031,583 yuan in cash reserves. The reserves include 7,351.95 taels of standard gold, calculated at a fixed price of 0.779 in accordance with Article 2 of the Customs Gold Exchange Coupon Regulations. The cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The result of this inspection is that the cash exceeds one-tenth of the quota and the guarantee is less than four-tenths of the quota, which is in line with the quantitative system. This report is hereby made. May 1, 1935, Li Fuxun, Chairman of the Supervisory Board of the Central Bank, Supervisors Xie Mingxun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, and Xu Jiqing.

Recent News from Wenzhou Baihao Condensed Milk Factory 159

Wenzhou Baihao Condensed Milk has been well-received by people across the country since its introduction to the market. This is because its production method is excellent, and the materials are pure, far surpassing imported goods. Monthly sales have reached thousands of cases. To expand its business, the factory has specially appointed Shanghai's well-reputed Jihua Tang Pharmacy as the national general manager to facilitate expansion and prevent leakage. The price is extremely cheap, with large tins priced at five dimes and small tins at one dime and three cents. Department stores, pharmacies, and other food stores across the country all sell it.

City Sounds 160

The Jue Lu Ballroom Newly Installed with Air Conditioning After Mr. Zhang Zhiqing took over the Jue Lu Ballroom, he hired experts to design and decorate it, so the interior has been completely renovated and is vastly different from the past. Although it has not been open for long, dance enthusiasts have been extraordinarily crowded every day. The ballroom is centrally located, the dancers are excellent, the music is clear and melodious, and the service is attentive, so it is no wonder that people from all walks of life flock to it. It is now reported that Mr. Zhang, in view of the increasingly hot weather in recent days and for the comfort of the dancers, has spared no expense to install the latest type of air conditioning system. It is currently being installed day and night and should be completed soon.

Longhu Rendan Selling Well In recent years, imports of foreign goods have been excessive. Patriotic people have taken measures to promote domestic goods. Domestic industries have also devoted themselves to research on their products. The Longhu Rendan produced by the Sino-French Pharmacy, with its excellent materials, has long been trusted by all sectors of society. Recently, with the weather getting hotter, sales of this medicine have increased sharply. Various institutions and groups are purchasing it in bulk for distribution as gifts. The Military Medical Department of the Ministry of National Defense recently ordered fifty large boxes. It is said that this is the first batch purchased by the city, and more will be purchased in large quantities in the future to meet the needs of the military. As a result, the pharmaceutical factory on Daxilu Road is adding workers and working day and night to produce it, which shows how popular this domestic product is.

Ma-Style Comedian Snake King Kun Performs in Mingzhu Since its opening, the Pengzhu Grand Theatre on Lao Baizi Road and Fusheng Road has been striving for improvement in all aspects. Recently, at great expense, it hired the famous Cantonese opera Ma-style comedian Snake King Kun from Guangdong to perform in Shanghai. The Ma style refers to the Ma Shizeng style, and Snake King Kun's skills are actually superior to Ma Shizeng's. Every time he appears on stage, he makes the audience burst into laughter. Snake King Kun's humor is not only apparent on the surface, but his underlying humor is even more thought-provoking. Since Cantonese opera was introduced to Shanghai, such a figure has never been seen. Coupled with the collaboration of the famous actress Guan Yinglian, it is even more perfect and difficult to match, so the theater has been sold out every day.

Weather Report 161

The Xujiahui Observatory issued the following weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday: Shandong and its surrounding areas are clear, with winds from the southeast to southwest, caused by a low pressure passing through Mongolia and moving east. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River are clear and still fine, gradually becoming less so and changing, with winds from the southeast to northeast. Ma'an Island, the south, and the East China Sea are overcast with rain, with fairly strong northeast to southeast winds. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 71.6 degrees and the lowest was 49.3 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 73.0 degrees and the lowest was 47.1 degrees.

Zhejiang's Fourth Provincial Games Opened Yesterday Track and Field Competition for Men and Women Began Yesterday, with Good Results and Several Provincial Records Broken 164

The opening ceremony of the Fourth Zhejiang Provincial Games was held at 8:00 AM yesterday at the Meidong Gaoqiao Provincial Stadium. The number of athletes participating in this year's games from various counties, cities, and schools is particularly large compared to previous years, totaling one hundred and twelve units and one thousand four hundred and ninety-nine male and female athletes, which shows that the promotion of sports in Zhejiang Province in recent years has gradually become popular. In addition, more than 20,000 guests and spectators attended. The ceremony was grand, and the atmosphere was enthusiastic. After the opening ceremony, the sports began at 9:00 AM. On that day, the Central Aviation School specially sent twelve aircraft to circle in the sky, scattering slogans for the games. The colors were vibrant, and the scene was dazzling. Moreover, the weather was overcast and clear, with a gentle breeze on the face. The athletes were full of energy, and the results were quite good.

Venue Arrangement The main entrance of the venue was hung with a white cloth banner reading "Zhejiang Fourth Provincial Games," with the couplet "Yue Kingdom's ambition, upright instruction; Wu Mountain's vigor, gathering heroes." The atmosphere was solemn. Inside the venue, there were the General Affairs Department, Reception Department, Judging Department, Press Room, First Aid Room, etc. The command room was located in the south, displaying awards from central dignitaries and various parties in the province. They were dazzling and beautiful, totaling more than three hundred items. Inside and outside the venue, there were also large contingents of military police and scouts from various schools maintaining order. The games did not charge admission, allowing people from all walks of life to visit freely. The order was generally tidy.

Attendees After 7:00 AM, various dignitaries arrived at the venue one after another, including Chairman of the Games and Provincial Chairman Huang Shaohong, Vice Chairman and Director of Education Xian Shaodi, Provincial Party Committee members Wang Jianyang, Fang Qingru, Wu Wangji, Hangzhou Mayor Zhou Xiangxian, Deputy Director of the Security Office Xuan Tiewu, Central Aviation School Principal Zhou Zhirou, Vice Principal Mao Bangchu, Director of Political Training Jiang Jianren, Defense School Principal Huang Zhenqiu, Zhejiang University Principal Guo Renyuan, National West Lake Art Academy Principal Lin Fengmian, Provincial Government Secretary-General Huang Huabiao, High Court President Zheng Wenti, Chief Prosecutor Zheng Tian, Highway Bureau Director Zhu Yaoting, and Telephone Bureau Director Zhao Huizeng, totaling dozens of people.

Chairman's Speech At the opening ceremony of the games, Chairman Huang Shaohong gave a speech, roughly saying that in this time of national crisis, if we want to save the country, we must first save ourselves. If we want to save ourselves, we must first strengthen our bodies. We must know that the significance of the games is not only in the length of individual competitions but is also of great importance to the strength of the country. In past games, 90% of the participants were students. It is hoped that all people in Zhejiang, men and women, young and old, will have the opportunity to participate and achieve the goal of physical fitness. He also said that in order to achieve good results, we must pay attention to sportsmanship and discipline, cultivate sportsmanship, friendly team discipline, and examine the progress of competition results, especially the progress in discipline.

Party Department Address Next, Xu Shaodi, Chairman of the Preparatory Committee, reported on the progress of the preparations and thanked all sectors of society. Xu then read a congratulatory telegram from Education Minister Wang Shijie. Finally, Fang Qingru, representative of the Provincial Party Department, gave an address, saying that attention should be paid to the diet and hygiene of the athletes from various schools, as they are related to sports performance.

Minister's Congratulatory Telegram The original text of Minister Wang's congratulatory telegram from the Ministry of Education reads: To Director Xu of the Hangzhou Education Department, forwarded to the Zhejiang Provincial Games Committee: I was very pleased to hear that your meeting will open on May 2. I hope that all the athletes will work hard to participate, and that discipline and various achievements can surpass past records, setting an example for the many scholars. Wang Shijie.

Tennis Performance After the opening ceremony, Provincial Chairman Huang Shaohong went to the tennis court for a tennis performance. Huang was paired with Shanghai's volleyball star Xu Heng as a team, while the opposing team was composed of Jiang Jianren, Director of Political Training at the Aviation School, and Xu Mingtao of the Air Force Special Party Department. The Huang-Xu team played with great spirit, creating a one-sided situation. As a result, the Huang-Xu team won six to one.

Globe Brand Bakelite Whistle Samples Offered 169

The Puji Electric Appliance Hardware Factory at 56 Sanzai Li, Jingxiu Road, Ximen, Shanghai, has created a Globe brand bakelite whistle (also known as a bakelite conductor's whistle). The material is sturdy and durable, the color is beautiful and lovely, and the blowing is light, accurate, and the sound is extremely loud. It can indeed achieve the effect of unified command, and it is of great benefit to mental health when used for a long time. Now is the time for sports meets to be held everywhere, and it is indeed an indispensable tool for referees and physical education teachers. The factory has now entrusted the Commercial Press, the China Bookstore, the Yixin Educational Supplies Company, and the Qinfen Bookstore as special managers. Recently, counterfeit and inferior goods have been discovered, crudely made and unusable. Please pay special attention to specifying the Globe trademark when purchasing to avoid being deceived. Out-of-towners can purchase from the local China Bookstore or Commercial Press branch for proper purchase. Sports people from all over the place, if they want to ask for samples, can attach 3.5 cents of postage stamps and send them directly to the factory, which will be sent by registered mail. Institutions, if more are needed, must be certified with a seal, limited to one dozen, postage stamps.

Their final defeat was due to the lack of endurance of his assistant, Hong Yukui, who had difficulty coping. Clarke's right hand and Bowes' left hand each showed superb skills, and they also focused on Hong's weaknesses, so they got their wish and won the doubles championship. In the first game, Zhu and Hong won easily with 21 to 13. The second and third games both failed at 19 points. The results of the two games were both 19 to 21, which is extremely regrettable.

China Sports Federation Men's and Women's Volleyball Schedule: Games Begin May 9 177

The regulations and schedule for this year's China School Sports Federation volleyball competition have been announced by the committee as follows:

(1) The competition adopts a group single round-robin system (men) with two groups, and the winners will play in the finals; (women) adopts a single round-robin system.

(2) The competition rules will be implemented in accordance with the latest published volleyball rules of the National Sports Association. Both men's and women's groups will adopt a best-of-three system, but the men's group finals will use a best-of-five system.

(3) The referees will be hired by the host team with the consent of the visiting team, or the host team will ask the China Referee Association to appoint them.

(4) In case of rain, the host team will try to borrow a gymnasium to hold the event, and no rescheduling is allowed.

(5) The registration form must be submitted to the chairman of the organizing committee (Mr. Chen De of Fudan University) no later than one day before the competition. The number of registered players is stipulated to be 12 for men and 15 for women.

(6) The location of the men's group finals and the referees will be determined by the committee.

(7) The competition time is 4:00 PM.

National Government Approves this Year's Shandong Province Education and Cultural Expenses 180

The National Government has approved the total amount of ordinary revenue and expenditure funds for Shandong Province in the 23rd year, each totaling 23,800,910 yuan. Among them, the education and cultural expenditure is 2,707,129 yuan (2,633,543 yuan in the previous year, an increase of 73,586 yuan), and the temporary expenses are 76,905 yuan (85,833 yuan in the previous year, a decrease of 8,928 yuan). The National Government, in accordance with Article 20 of the principles of the financial revenue and expenditure system recently approved by the Central Political Council, clearly stipulates that the total amount of funds related to education, culture, economic construction, health, medical treatment, childcare, and relief should be at least 60 percent of the total budget in the provinces and regions. It has ordered the Executive Yuan and other institutions to instruct the province to increase this ratio as much as possible to support the country's efforts to build up its strength and educate its people.

Tidbits 185

— (Ji Chengxing)

The three stages of life: When you are young, you want grandma; when you are old, you want a woman; when you are old, you want a coffin.

Everyone has their strengths: a bald head is convenient for drilling, big feet are convenient for climbing, quick hands are convenient for stealing, and a vicious heart is convenient for dealing with the world!

The cause and effect of gain and loss: With money, you have women; with women, you have love. When love is lost, women run away, and the money bag is empty.

Snobbishness oppresses people: Snobbish people are cultivated by people without snobbishness. People without snobbishness are oppressed by people with snobbishness, and they are willing to do so. Don't you hear such boring words: "It is an honor to be slapped by ××!"

Love and Bread 186

— Hu Tianyu

Love is the wave of life. Where there is life, there is love, just like where there is the sea, there are waves. Bread is the sustenance of life. Where there is life, there must be bread, just like fish need water.

Love is spiritual food, while bread is material nourishment.

People cannot lose material nourishment, just as fish cannot live without water. Fish leave the water and can lose their lives in an instant; people lose material nourishment and can turn a strong body into steamed buns in an instant.

But sometimes people may as well lose spiritual food, just as the sea may as well be calm sometimes. The sea has no waves, although it loses its activity and its greatness, it is still the sea; people have no spiritual food, although they feel dull and boring, they are still human beings.

Therefore, life may as well be without love, but it cannot be without bread!

What's more, love is often built on bread. Without bread, you can't even protect your life, let alone love. Let us sing the popular song now: "Hurry up and throw it away, knead the fresh flowers, throw away the fresh flowers, close the heart flowers, collect the flowers of love, forget him, don't think about him, unlock the locks and shackles!" It can be seen that love is just to sell the shackles, it is not as tasty as bread.

What the masses need now is not love, but bread!

Ghost Cry 187

— Chonglou

I am not a scientist, but I still have a non-superstitious mind. I don't believe in "ghosts" because I have never seen a ghost.

But recently I have often heard a kind of terrible sound—like the ghost cry described by people who talk about "ghosts"! This sound comes from police cars and ambulances. Sometimes it suddenly vibrates in the air, passes by the windows along the road, and pierces my eardrums very loudly.

It is said that this is a special device on the police car that can make pedestrians avoid it when they hear it; perhaps it is precisely because its sound is too peculiar that I named it "ghost cry".

How is this not a "ghost cry"? When you hear that sound, you will know that a theft has occurred, and you will immediately think of the scene of catching thieves, fighting, and many deaths and injuries; or a car accident has occurred, and you will immediately think of the tragic scene of pedestrians being crushed under the wheels, with broken feet and legs, and blood flowing from the brain; although you only hear the terrible sound, it is as if you witnessed the terrible everything.

The city is a place of murder, and this "ghost cry" is just a report, no matter which aspect the report belongs to.

I wonder what people living in the city think about this increasing "ghost cry" sound?

After the Hunter Runs Out of Bullets 188

— Author

Little Western Paradise 189

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter 12: Ashamed of Having No Clothes, I Hang Curtains to Avoid Guests; Industrious in Saving Lamp Oil, I Copy Before Dawn

Zhou Yourong said, "The classrooms are all so simple. Of course, other facilities are out of the question." Zhiqian shook his head and said, "Speaking of this, one can truly shed tears for the people of the Northwest. They lack all the tools for studying, to put it simply. How can we talk about any equipment? An hour after my conversation with the principal, that teacher went to the classroom to teach arithmetic. He spent a lot of effort explaining things like how many catties and taels are in a ton, copying it on the blackboard. The students were even busier. Because they didn't have books, everyone was copying from their notebooks. Since the students had to listen to the lecture and also copy the book, they couldn't manage it. Therefore, they had to wait until after the lecture before starting to copy. While the students were copying, the teacher would stop lecturing. In the end, the teacher finished lecturing and dismissed the class. The students, because it was getting late, didn't have time to finish copying, so they closed the classroom, in order to preserve the chalk writing on the blackboard and copy it again tomorrow, so it wouldn't be rubbed off. At that time, I also said goodbye and left, arranging to talk again tomorrow. But my curiosity was strong, so the next day I got up very early and went to see them when their first class started, in order to confirm whether they were attending class on time. Fortunately, there was no gatekeeper there, so as long as the main gate was open, I could enter without hesitation. The people of the Northwest are very good at getting up early, so even though I got up very early to go, they had already opened the gate." (195)

Rectification of Peculiar Surnames 190

— Yu Hua

The special issue on peculiar surnames in this column on the 27th can be described as diverse and spectacular. However, it seems inappropriate to include the surnames of the Peking opera circle among the peculiar ones in Mr. Yijiao's discussion. This is because, in the Qing Dynasty, Manchus all used their given names as surnames, almost to the point of one person, one surname. If we consider them strange, we couldn't record them all. (For example, Puyi used Pu as his surname, the previous generation used Zai, (Zai Zhen) used Zai as his surname, and the generation before that used Yi, (Yikuang) used Yi as his surname.) After the change of dynasty, many adopted Han surnames. As for Shi Huibao, Gong Dayuan, En Xiaofeng, Rui Debao, De Junru, Ci Ruiquan, Ru Fuhui, etc., I know that they are all Manchus.

Furthermore, Ru Fuhui sings Xiaomian (a type of comedic role), not Qingyi (a leading female role), and together with his brother Fu Lan, who studies Wusheng (male martial role), they both came from the Fu Liancheng opera school and are the sons of the famous Qin player Ru Laiqing, also from a family of performers.

Records of Lingering Imperial Incense 191

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

In terms of consumer value and use, socks are of course a smaller item than phoenix shoes, and no matter how meticulous one is, one cannot find any patterns to be meticulous about on socks. Therefore, the palace had not established a separate sock-making industry but instead let the shoemakers take charge of it concurrently. Even so, the Empress Dowager paid special attention to her own socks and was very picky. She had to change into a new pair of socks every day, and after taking them off, she would never use them again. In her eyes, a pair of socks was really worthless, like a thread! But in all conscience, her socks were indeed valuable! Their raw material was the finest pure white soft silk, and the workmanship was even more exquisite, making them so suitable for Her Old Majesty's honorable feet that they were almost perfectly fitted everywhere. Even the silk stockings we wear now would not easily achieve such results, let alone things made by human hands at that time?

Each sock must have two seams, one in the front and one in the back. This is because socks made of soft silk are not as elastic as modern thread or silk socks, so these two seams must be opened on the sock leg; otherwise, how would people's feet fit in? However, from an aesthetic point of view, these two seams cannot be considered a major defect. The Empress Dowager, who loved beauty the most, would of course try her best to remedy this defect. So, those skilled needleworkers came up with an excellent solution for her: they used silk threads of various colors to tie special patterns around the two seams, thus hiding the two seams and making them look like part of the pattern. (305)

Vegetable Rice 192

— Tian Sheweng

It's lunchtime: small restaurants on the street are cooking fragrant "vegetable rice" in woks. White, pearl-like rice, fresh green vegetables, stir-fried with lard – this is called "vegetable rice."

A plate of spare ribs, a bowl of egg flower soup, eaten with vegetable rice: this is called "spare rib vegetable rice." Two large pieces of meat, a bowl of pickled vegetable soup, eaten with vegetable rice: this is called "four-joy vegetable rice." There's also shredded pork fried rice, shrimp fried rice, gizzard and liver fried rice, large meat noodles, eel noodles, shredded pork fried rice cake, wontons... small restaurants have everything to offer for friends from writing offices to choose from.

Wontons and meat noodles are "snacks" and are not filling enough, so they are often eaten as lunch. Eating at restaurants every day is beyond the means of most writing office friends. Considering the price is cheap and it fills you up, "vegetable rice" is the thing to have.

Most writing office friends don't have room and board provided. Garret rooms and lofts are their residences; eating becomes a problem. Due to economic reasons, they have to have a special relationship with "vegetable rice."

When it's lunchtime, one person after another comes from writing offices to vegetable rice restaurants – this is the reason.

The ancients said: "With full vegetable rice, even coarse clothes feel soft." Friends who eat writing office meals, in principle, absolutely cannot wear coarse clothes; at the very least, they must have one or two sets of Western suits. As for whether this kind of "vegetable rice" is filling or not, that's another question!

The Editorial Department

Miscellaneous Talks

Beheading 193

— Zhen Lu

But hearing the locals curse people with "kill your skull," and the notoriously shrewd Ningbo people curse with "chop your head off," and most other people also use beheading as a curse, it can be seen that almost everyone with a head dislikes beheading and would rarely be fooled by Jin Shengtan's wild statement that "beheading is the most enjoyable thing in the world."

I have thought that the ancients established the crime of beheading probably to exert the effect of eliminating life; but regardless of which part of the human body the perpetrator of the crime or trouble belongs to, all the blame is attributed to a head and it is made to bear the burden of compensation. Isn't it too unfair to single out the head for such treatment?

In the past, the executioners who carried out the beheading of criminals in our country could not be employed unless they were skilled in the art of killing, so the job of beheading was regarded as a profession, and some were hereditary. Since the Republic of China, these executioners have become unemployed. Even if the warlords of a certain period could not bear the true talent to be lost and the national art to decline, and intended to promote them, I am afraid there would also be sighs of talent being difficult to find.

In the past, after the supervising executioner carried out the execution, he would definitely go to the City God Temple to burn incense, called "shedding the shadow." After returning to the yamen, he would have to ascend to the official seat, and a group of runners and yamen servants would hold sticks and boards and shout to drive him in and out, called "arranging the yamen." The intention was to fear that the head was killed unjustly, or that the vengeful spirit would not dissipate and would immediately chase after the supervising executioner to harass him for his life, so it was necessary to trouble a colleague—the City God, who was the underworld authority—to lock up or drive away that uninteresting vengeful spirit. After killing his head, they were still afraid that his soul would be wronged and seek revenge. This kind of imposing but timid superstition could only be done by the officials of the past.

Nowadays, countries with a civilized appearance like to promote humanitarianism, legislating to retain the death penalty but abolish beheading, and even extend compassion to the remains, even stipulating the crime of damaging corpses, which is truly the extreme of compassion! But alas, the world is still chaotic, and the authorities also believe that severe laws must be used to govern unruly people, so the farce of beheading is again being publicly staged in what is considered an extraordinary state—recently, Russia even borrowed talent from abroad, inviting a Mr. Li from our country to replace a previous executioner who went insane and was suspended from duty. Germany also had two female spies and a romantic woman recently sentenced to beheading by the government, showing the trend of the revival of beheading in the world—those regarded as unruly people unexpectedly get to enjoy the taste of beheading, and people with a lust for killing also get to enjoy this unexpected spectacle in the 20th century.

Before the establishment of the National Government, I once visited Suzhou and was sitting in a rickshaw passing through a certain city gate when I inadvertently looked up and saw two lifelike human heads hanging high on top of the city gate. I was both surprised and disgusted, and had an indescribable feeling that surpassed the rare curiosity. I really didn't want to look at it any more, but my body had to pass under those two heads to enter the city. Since then, whenever I hear or see the word "beheading," the impression of those two heads on the Suzhou city gate inevitably resurfaces in my mind. I want to thank the official who presided over the killing and ordering for giving me such a deep and indelible impression, even though I have no luck to witness the spectacle of beheading! Amen!

Commercial News

Finance Yesterday, the Market's Gold Standard Supplemented Short Positions Fiercely, Rising by Twenty-Nine Yuan Seven Cents 194

Printing Silver Frequently Contracted, Foreign Exchange Was Extremely Tight, the Future Market Reached 800 Yuan

The Day Before, the Cantonese Syndicate Supplemented Short Positions, and the Exchange Market Was Average, Only at One Yuan

Since the Cantonese Syndicate's short covering the day before, the chips have become narrower, and people are eagerly optimistic. The Jewish merchant Qiao Zhifu secretly covered his short positions very fiercely. The frequent decline in printed silver and the extremely tight foreign exchange market contributed greatly to buying sentiment, rebounding to the 800-yuan mark. In the early morning, due to the decline in overseas silver markets and the reduction in the Montevideo forward silver price by 2.15 to 2.7 cents, and a slight increase in foreign exchange rates, the rise in London raw gold by 4 pence, people were in a cheerful mood. The over-the-counter pre-market trading opened, immediately rising to 74.5 yuan. The chips were even scarcer, rising again to 78.9 yuan. The Central Bank's official exchange rates were announced, with English and American currencies remaining flat. The customs gold unit rose by 3 cents, and the gold standard price rose to 829 yuan. The market opened with a high price, remaining normal after the opening, hovering around 80 yuan. HSBC's official English and American exchange rates remained flat. In addition, the Central Bank and Sassoon continued to hold shillings, leading to a period of weakness. However, with people tending towards optimism and the market being exhausted, it was easy to pull up. Chinese merchants vigorously bought foreign exchange, contributing greatly to buying sentiment, gradually rising. Reuters reported that speculators believed the U.S. government's delay in purchasing silver was extremely unfavorable to speculators and that multiple opinions, such as raising the silver price to $1.29, seemed to indicate a need to reduce the silver coin fineness. This stirred people's hearts. The Cantonese and Dalian syndicates bought up U.S. dollars, gradually breaking through 90 yuan. There were also rumors that the Jewish merchant Qiao Zhifu was buying up U.S. dollars. The foreign exchange market became even tighter, and buying sentiment was even stronger, once rising to 798 yuan. Sassoon and the banks seized the opportunity to sell at high prices, leading to a reversal in the afternoon, but the market remained firm after the close. The future market was boosted by the report of a reduction in printed silver by 26 annas, fueling buying and rising again after opening. However, because the banks fiercely sold at high prices and engaged in hedging activities, the market tended to decline, but did not break the 90-yuan mark. There was continued support at the low price, and the market gradually stabilized after the low. Later, the silver price fell again by 10 annas for the second time, leading to another rebound. The consumption of spot cotton is unusually quiet. Manufacturers do not handle high-priced raw cotton due to the decline in yarn prices. The source of Tonghua is 278 bales. Shandong American cotton 47.00. Shenxin Factory took delivery of 200 pieces of spot goods and sent them to the factory.

Special Margin Increased for Standard Cotton This Month

For the May contract of standard cotton, the Chinese Merchants Yarn and Cloth Exchange will increase the special margin by 3 yuan per dan for new sales and purchases made from May 1, and charge both deposit accounts.

Recent Two Days of Imported Cotton 200

Calm and Without Characteristics

Tuesday, April 30: At the opening of the US cotton market, each month rose and fell by 1-3 points. The market situation was stagnant. Dealers waited and watched. First, it was firm due to the rise in silver prices in London and Monterrey, and then it returned due to long covering and the weak stock and wheat markets. There were showers in West Texas and Oklahoma. In the afternoon, the Bombay gang bought in, and dealers paid attention to the July contract. Current demand was not good, and there were not many sellers. The ground was still firm. The textile industry was bleak. The closing was flat. The spot price did not move, and the futures rose and fell by 1 point. English spot price rose 3 points, and futures fell 1-2 points. Indian cotton speculators bought in, and European exporters bought in old cotton and sold new cotton, saying that Pingguoer fell flat to Robbie, Aomula rose 1.5-2 Robbie, and Bai Luoxi rose 1.77-3 Robbie.

Wednesday, May 1: At the opening of the US cotton market, it was calm and without characteristics. The transaction volume was not large, and the market price rose and fell by 1-2 points. Dealers needed old cotton, but buyers were still doubtful before the government's policy on new cotton was developed. In the afternoon, New Orleans sold out, and long positions were closed out, slightly weakening. It quickly recovered. Spot goods were firm, but buyers were wary because prices were already high. It is rumored that the Cotton Cooperative Society intends to borrow from the government to store cotton and return it with new cotton futures. The closing was stable. The spot price fell 5 points, and the futures fell 1-5 points. English cotton spot and futures both rose 2 points. Indian cotton old cotton was lacking, but European exporters sold a large amount of new cotton. As a result, Pingguoer rose by 0.5 Robbie, Aomula fell by 0.75-1 Robbie, and Bai Luoxi fell by 0.75-2 Robbie. The original telegram records on the left:

Grain: The Weakness of the Flour Futures Market Gradually Subsides 201

After the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices for each month were initially weak and then stabilized. The quoted prices for imported wheat were lower by 0.4 yuan in Chicago and lower by 0.48 yuan in Canada. At the time of opening, due to the good flour sales the day before, sentiment was strong, and the prices were up by about 0.03 yuan compared to the closing prices at the end of the previous month. However, it was heard that major factories had booked three ships of imported wheat due to its cheapness, with prices rumored to be 4.69 yuan or 4.71 yuan. Therefore, yesterday's market sentiment was affected by this, and the opening prices showed weakness, falling by about 0.01-0.02 yuan compared to the previous day. By the opening of the afternoon market, although the sales to customers in the north were not as strong as at the end of the month, they were still continuing, with an estimated 30,000-40,000 bags. Therefore, sentiment for the current month recovered and stabilized. The far months also showed slight improvement due to the rebound in gold prices. Looking ahead, if there are opportunities to continue booking imported wheat, the market should stabilize temporarily. As a result, the current month was down 0.025 yuan, May was down 0.01 yuan, July was down 0.005 yuan, August was unchanged, September was down 0.025 yuan, and October was up 0.021 yuan.
